## Answer

**Materially significant update for this automation turn (JanРђ»10,Рђ»2026):**

**Cursor 2.0 with proprietary Composer model released**  
РъА№ИЈ Cursor has shipped **CursorРђ»2.0**, introducing its **first inРђЉhouse LLM named *Composer***, positioned as a highРђЉspeed coding model with substantially faster task turnaround and multiРђЉagent workflows. The update also formally adds **isolated multiРђЉagent execution** using strategies like Git worktrees or remote execution to avoid file conflicts when running parallel agents. ЬѕђciteЬѕѓturn0news0Ьѕѓturn0news2ЬѕЂ

**Why this counts as a major change**
Рђб **New proprietary model (Composer):** This is CursorРђЎs first internal LLM rather than relying solely on external providers. ЬѕђciteЬѕѓturn0news2ЬѕЂ  
Рђб **Parallel agent support:** Up to eight agents can work concurrently on a codebase in isolated workspaces, addressing a key workflow advance. ЬѕђciteЬѕѓturn0news0ЬѕЂ  
Рђб **Performance shift:** Cursor emphasizes large speed gains in typical coding tasks with the new model. ЬѕђciteЬѕѓturn0news2ЬѕЂ

Рђб **Claude Code:** No publicly documented new major release or feature launch in the monitoring period matching your criteria since the last notification. No new agentic model announcement surfaced in search results.

**Implication:** Cursor now supports **persistent cloudРђЉexecuting agents** with handoff from local CLI, enhancing asynchronous workflows.

**Parallel Agents & Worktrees (Docs Рђћ no new release but still relevant):**
- Multiple local agents can run in parallel. ЬѕђciteЬѕѓturn0search19ЬѕЂ

**Summary:** *Significant functional update in agent modes and cloud handoff.*
